[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe function `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` within `lib/ftp.c` when processing a crafted FTP[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMDTM response.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type: Memory safety violation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mglobal-buffer-overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Trigger: A single test input supplied to `curl_fuzzer_ftp` caused an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately past a globally allocated buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Curl_seconds` in `parsedate.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer report:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Error location: `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m2107:21[0m[39m` inside `ftp_state_mdtm_resp`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Faulting address is [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes past a [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m-byte global array [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Curl_seconds`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Stack trace highlights FTP state machine routines and the fuzzing entry point [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `curl_fuzzer.cc`.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzz harness context:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer was run with libFuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in interactive mode.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The failure emerged during the FTP command/response handling path [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`ftp_statemachine` → `Curl_pp_statemach` → `ftp_multi_statemach` → `ftp_doing`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow occurs on a global buffer, not on heap or stack.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The global buffer in question is defined in `lib/parsedate.c` and represents [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed date components.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The violation happens when handling an MDTM [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmodify time[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m response from the FTP[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserver.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to inspect for a holistic view:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `lib/ftp.c`, function `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2107[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Examine how [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `lib/ftp.c`, function `ftp_statemachine` and related FTP state‐machine logic. [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. `lib/parsedate.c`, definition and size of the global `Curl_seconds` array.  [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Scope for further analysis:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and isolate the root cause:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow arises because ftp_213_date currently treats a second‐value of [0m[1;36m60[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mleap second[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as valid, yet later code unconditionally indexes [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, where `Curl_seconds` has only [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. When `tm->tm_sec == [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m`, this lookup overflows the global array.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch the bounds check in ftp_213_date:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open lib/ftp.c and locate the function `ftp_213_date` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2021[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change the conditional that currently reads:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*month > [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*day > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*hour > [0m[1;36m23[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*minute > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*second > [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return FALSE;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to enforce seconds ≤ [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*month > [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*day > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*hour > [0m[1;36m23[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*minute > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*second > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return FALSE;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that any MDTM response yielding a seconds field of [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m is rejected[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the parser and never propagated to the formatter.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve existing state‐machine behavior:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Because `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` only formats the time when `ftp_213_date` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns TRUE, tightening the bound on `*second` simply causes invalid or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleap‐second responses to take the existing “else” or error‐handling path. No [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream logic is modified.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild and validate:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Recompile curl with standard test suite and the FTP fuzzer harness.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `make test` and the `curl_fuzzer_ftp` fuzz target under AddressSanitizer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto confirm the global‐buffer‐overflow no longer occurs.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that valid MDTM responses with seconds in [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m continue to be correctly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed and formatted.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side‐effect considerations:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only rejected inputs are those with “[0m[1;36m60[0m[39m” seconds, which correspond to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleap‐second timestamps. As FTP’s MDTM extension uses standard UT time without leap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds, rejecting [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m is protocol‐compliant and safer than risking memory [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorruption.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to external libraries, fuzz harnesses, or tests. The fix [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis localized to the parsing logic and preserves all existing functionality for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid inputs.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis minimal change prevents out‐of‐bounds indexing into `Curl_seconds` while [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretaining full support for [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m seconds and ensures the FTP state‐machine logic and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests remain unaffected.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma global-buffer-overflow in the function `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `lib/ftp.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_seconds` defined in `parsedate.c`. A patch was attempted in `lib/ftp.c` to [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`> [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m` to `> [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m`. After rebuilding and rerunning the fuzzer, the same [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mglobal-buffer-overflow remains at the same code location.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During fuzzing with libFuzzer, AddressSanitizer reports a [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mglobal-buffer-overflow in `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` at:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     READ of size [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m at [0m[1;36m0x[0m[33m...[0m[39m is located [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after global variable [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'Curl_seconds'[0m[39m [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       defined in [0m[32m'parsedate.c:113'[0m[39m of size [0m[1;36m480[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     SUMMARY: AddressSanitizer: global-buffer-overflow [0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m2107:21[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows the overflow is triggered by handling an MDTM response [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the FTP state machine.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The global buffer `Curl_seconds` in `parsedate.c` is being indexed or read [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond its allocated bounds.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `lib/ftp.c`, around line [0m[1;36m2019[0m[39m, the code validates date/time fields parsed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the MDTM response:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*month > [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*day > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*hour > [0m[1;36m23[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*minute > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*second > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return FALSE;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change prevents “[0m[1;36m60[0m[39m” from being accepted as a valid second value.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Result After Patch  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - AddressSanitizer reports the identical overflow at [0m                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m:    [0m[32m"fifty"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fifty-one"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fifty-two"[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m130[0m[39m:    [0m[32m"fifty-three"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fifty-four"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fifty-five"[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m131[0m[39m:    [0m[32m"fifty-six"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fifty-seven"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fifty-eight"[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m132[0m[39m:    [0m[32m"fifty-nine"[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m133[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The global-buffer-overflow arises in ftp_state_mdtm_resp when it [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally indexes Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[39m. Although the raw MDTM parser [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisallows seconds >[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m, subsequent use of right/UTC gmtime can set tm_sec to [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegal leap‐second value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Curl_seconds has only [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m entries [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so indexing at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m overruns the array.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter harness or fuzzing logic.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to reject malformed “second” fields at parse time [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevious patch in ftp_213_date[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must still use Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m for human-readable formatting.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m or other date routines elsewhere.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In lib/ftp.c, inside ftp_state_mdtm_resp, immediately after the Curl_gmtime [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2093[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, clamp tm->tm_sec to the valid range [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Steps[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate ftp_state_mdtm_resp in lib/ftp.c:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        const struct tm *tm = &buffer;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mputenv[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32mTZ[0m[32m=[0m[32mright[0m[32m/UTC"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        result = [0m[1;35mCurl_gmtime[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfiletime, &buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return result;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Insert after the gmtime call:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Prevent indexing past Curl_seconds: clamp leap-second [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          struct tm *mutable_tm = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct tm *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m&buffer;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmutable_tm->tm_sec > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            mutable_tm->tm_sec = [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the existing msnprintf call intact:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        headerbuflen = [0m[1;35mmsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheaderbuf, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheaderbuf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[32m"... %s seconds GMT\r\n"[0m[39m,[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure no other changes to header formatting, parsing logic, harness code, or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal data.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Clamping tm_sec bounds prevents out-of-range indexing and eliminates the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mASan-reported overflow.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach is minimal and localized: it only affects ftp_state_mdtm_resp, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving all existing FTP state‐machine and date‐parsing logic.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It respects the previous parse-time check for “second” >[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mftp_213_date[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile addressing the downstream leap-second case introduced by gmtime.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No tests or harness code are modified, so existing tests and fuzz targets [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to function.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A true leap-second [0m[1;39m([0m[33mtm_sec[0m[39m==[0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is displayed as “fifty-nine seconds,” which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslightly underreports by one second. In practice, this is acceptable for formatting[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFTP “Last-Modified” headers; clients do not expect leap-second granularity.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a future requirement arises to display “sixty seconds,” the array [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCurl_seconds could be extended with a “sixty” entry. That would be a separate [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menhancement, but is not required to prevent the overflow.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References to Similar Code[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other code paths in curl clamp month/day/hour bounds before use [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. in date [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This patch follows the same defensive‐clamping pattern.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
